[30;1m222 | [0m[35mHTTP/2 defines a complex flow control system that uses a sliding window of[0m
[30;1m223 | [0m[35mdata on both a per-stream and per-connection basis. Essentially, each[0m

[30;1m228 | [0m[35mstream (causing the window for that stream to be opened), or on stream ``0``,[0m
